[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA heap-use-after-free vulnerability was detected in the XZ Utils library during [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing of the `fuzz_encode_stream` target. The issue occurs in the [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`compute_tree_checksum` function within the Tree checksum implementation [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`treeck.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, where memory is being accessed after it has been freed. The [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability has a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m51[0m[39m and involves an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte read operation on [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfreed heap memory.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Nature of the Vulnerability[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a heap-use-after-free vulnerability, a critical memory safety issue where [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe program attempts to read from a heap-allocated memory region after it has been [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeallocated. Specifically, the issue manifests as an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte read operation at [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddress `[0m[1;36m0x5060000000a0[0m[39m`, which is located [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m bytes inside a previously freed [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m56[0m[39m-byte memory region.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Call Stack Analysis[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is triggered through the following execution path:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Entry Point**: The fuzzer calls `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fuzz_encode_stream.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m81[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Encoding Pipeline**: The call progresses through `fuzz_code` → `lzma_code` → [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`stream_encode` → `block_encode`[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Checksum Computation**: The issue occurs in `lzma_check_update` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m143[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich calls `lzma_tree` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m100[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Vulnerability Site**: The actual heap-use-after-free occurs in [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`compute_tree_checksum` at line [0m[1;36m79[0m[39m in `[0m[35m/src/xz/src/liblzma/check/[0m[95mtreeck.c[0m[39m`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Memory Allocation Timeline[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe AddressSanitizer report reveals the lifecycle of the problematic memory region:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Allocation**: Memory was allocated via `malloc` in the `create_tree` function [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat line [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m of `treeck.c`[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Deallocation**: The memory was freed in `compute_tree_checksum` at line [0m[1;36m90[0m[39m of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`treeck.c`[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Invalid Access**: The same memory location was subsequently accessed at line [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m of `treeck.c`[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNotably, the stack trace shows that `compute_tree_checksum` appears multiple times [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the deallocation path, suggesting recursive calls where the function frees [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory and then attempts to access it in a parent or subsequent invocation.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Recursive Pattern**: The stack trace indicates `compute_tree_checksum` calling[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mitself recursively [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m82[0m[39m shown twice in the freed-by trace[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which may be [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelated to tree traversal operations[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Tree Data Structure**: The function names [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`create_tree`, [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`compute_tree_checksum`, `lzma_tree`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m suggest this is part of a tree-based checksum[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malgorithm implementation[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Consistent Reproducibility**: The fuzzer reports running the test case [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtimes with consistent failure, indicating this is a deterministic bug rather than a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrace condition[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcoordinates block encoding[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Data Structure Analysis**:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The tree data structure implementation and its memory management strategy[0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The ownership and lifetime semantics of tree nodes during checksum computation[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Algorithm Flow**:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The recursive tree traversal algorithm in `compute_tree_checksum`[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How the algorithm manages temporary tree structures[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The interaction between tree creation and checksum computation during the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mencoding process[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability appears to be in the core tree checksum computation logic, where [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/liblzma/check/treeck.h:[0m[1;36m14[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m16[0m                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m14[0m[39m:#define STATE_CLEAR   [0m[1;36m0[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m15[0m[39m:#define STATE_VISITED [0m[1;36m1[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m16[0m[39m:#define STATE_HASHED  [0m[1;36m2[0m                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe heap-use-after-free vulnerability occurs in the `compute_tree_checksum` [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction in `src/liblzma/check/treeck.c`. The issue stems from improper handling of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe state machine when traversing a cyclic graph structure:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**The Problem:**[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `create_tree` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m51[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m53[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m creates backlinks to parent nodes under [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecific conditions, forming directed cycles rather than a pure tree structure[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `compute_tree_checksum` function uses a three-state machine [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSTATE_CLEAR → [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSTATE_VISITED → STATE_HASHED[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to handle cycles[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m69[0m[39m only checks for `STATE_HASHED` before returning early, missing the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`STATE_VISITED` check[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- When a cycle causes re-entry into a node that is currently `STATE_VISITED`:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The condition at line [0m[1;36m77[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode->state == STATE_CLEAR[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m fails[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The code falls through to lines [0m[1;36m89[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m90[0m[39m and frees the node[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - However, the original call that marked the node as `STATE_VISITED` is still [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mactive and executing its loop at line [0m[1;36m79[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - When the original call continues to the next edge iteration, it accesses [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`node->edge_count` on the already-freed memory[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - This triggers the heap-use-after-free detected at line [0m[1;36m79[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39maccessing offset [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the freed [0m[1;36m56[0m[39m-byte allocation[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Execution Trace Example:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mGraph: A → B → C → A [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbacklink[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. [0m[1;35mcompute_tree_checksum[0m[1;39m([0m[39mA, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: STATE_CLEAR → STATE_VISITED[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Enter loop at line [0m[1;36m79[0m[39m, process edge [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mB[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. [0m[1;35mcompute_tree_checksum[0m[1;39m([0m[39mB, [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: STATE_CLEAR → STATE_VISITED[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Process edge [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mC[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. [0m[1;35mcompute_tree_checksum[0m[1;39m([0m[39mC, [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: STATE_CLEAR → STATE_VISITED[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Process edge [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mA - backlink[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. [0m[1;35mcompute_tree_checksum[0m[1;39m([0m[39mA, [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: STATE_VISITED[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m69[0m[39m: Check fails [0m[1;39m([0m[39monly checks STATE_HASHED, not STATE_VISITED[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m77[0m[39m: Check fails [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate != STATE_CLEAR[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Lines [0m[1;36m89[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m90[0m[39m: FREE A ← Node A freed while still on call stack![0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Return to C, mark HASHED, free C[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Return to B, mark HASHED, free B  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Return to original A call at line [0m[1;36m79[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Continue loop: [0m[33mi[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, access node->edge_count ← USE-AFTER-FREE![0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Proposed Fix[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File:** `src/liblzma/check/treeck.c`  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Function:** `compute_tree_checksum`  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Line:** [0m[1;36m69[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change:**[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Current [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuggy[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!node || node->state == STATE_HASHED[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Fixed:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!node || node->state == STATE_VISITED || node->state == STATE_HASHED[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmore explicit[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!node || node->state != STATE_CLEAR[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix Justification[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This Fix is Optimal:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Change:** Single line modification that adds the missing state check[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves Algorithm Intent:** The state machine was designed to handle cycles;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis fix completes the implementation[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Correct Semantics:** [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - STATE_VISITED means [0m[32m"node is currently being processed on the call stack"[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Returning early prevents premature freeing and double-counting in checksum[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The node will be freed by its original [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutermost[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m recursive call when [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing completes[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Behavioral Changes:** Cycles already return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m contribution to checksum; [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis fix ensures they do so safely[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Safe Memory Management:** Each node is freed exactly once by the call that [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginally marked it as STATE_VISITED[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How It Preserves Existing Logic:**[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Tree Creation:** No changes to `create_tree` or backlink logic[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Checksum Computation:** Maintains the same checksum values [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcycles contribute [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **State Transitions:** Preserves CLEAR → VISITED → HASHED progression[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **API Contract:** `lzma_tree` behavior unchanged from caller perspective[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Streaming Support:** Works correctly with multiple calls via [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`lzma_check_update`[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How It Addresses the Evaluation Report:**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Heap-use-after-free at line [0m[1;36m79[0m[39m:** Fixed by preventing premature freeing of [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSTATE_VISITED nodes[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Memory freed at line [0m[1;36m90[0m[39m:** Now only executed when node is not on the call [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Recursive pattern:** Properly handles cycles without use-after-free or [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minfinite recursion[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Consistent reproducibility:** Fix eliminates the deterministic bug[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects and Mitigation:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **[0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m Expected:** The fix completes the intended state machine behavior[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Memory Leaks:** Not possible - all nodes still reach STATE_HASHED and get [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfreed by their original call[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Checksum Values:** Unchanged - cycles already returned [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, now they do so [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafely[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Performance:** Negligible impact - adds one comparison to an existing [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcondition[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix follows the pattern used in `src/liblzma/common/index.[0m[1;92mc:193[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m207[0m[39m` for the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`index_tree_node_end` function, which uses post-order traversal [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprocess children [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore freeing parent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without cycles. Our fix ensures that nodes with cycles are [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malso freed safely by preventing freeing while the node is still in use on the call [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Implementation Notes[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix must be applied to the initial codebase in `src/liblzma/check/treeck.c` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat line [0m[1;36m69[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes needed to header files, test files, or other components[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix is self-contained and does not affect the broader codebase[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Existing tests should pass without modification[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer should no longer trigger this vulnerability after the fix[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
